5: DO NOT SPAM POST CREATIONS
Please don't post images to creations or #contest-creations that are:
    • Low effort (these include, but are not limited to: youtube tutorials, singular block builds).
    • Reference images of a creation that you're building.
    • Screenshots of your creation's block count.
    • Creations that are not yours.
    • Creations that are a WIP. Please post these in creations-feedback.
